class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7572044584f4349f602c529fe8511ede_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7572044584f4349f602c529fe8511ede_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><br/><br/>长期受老美牵制，也是非常不爽的。1964年，巴拿马政府跟当时的肯尼迪政府达成协议，其中一项是在运河上同时升起美国和巴拿马国旗。<br/><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-dd4cf823f35ae7bd2a9cdc9f64f1a362_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"990\" data-rawheight=\"660\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-dd4cf823f35ae7bd2a9cdc9f64f1a362_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><br/><br/>从老美手里收回运河的管辖权，并不容易。1989年，美国侵略巴拿马<br/><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8dd3fbdb98b89967636663c8753b6f82_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><br/><br/>截至2015年，<b>巴拿马运河给巴拿马政府带来5亿美元的经济收益。</b>巴拿马也成了巴西、智利以后，拉美经济最发达的国家。<br/><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3179d420524796dda5d6c24682556b82_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"600\" data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-eb728cd7a8f79e98ac5b44d8188e09b1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"596\" data-rawheight=\"338\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-eb728cd7a8f79e98ac5b44d8188e09b1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><br/><br/>尽管如此，一条运河的吞吐量毕竟有限，巴拿马运河的航运可以说已经饱和了。<br/><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf6a4f6edc20e2f629df840a944fe805_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"400\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf6a4f6edc20e2f629df840a944fe805_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg width=&#39;482&#39; height=&#39;656&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"482\" data-rawheight=\"656\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"482\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-28ae20ab4451b42547264b7e171e085e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-28ae20ab4451b42547264b7e171e085e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而且，还是墨西哥人家门口的世界杯。2002年，韩国还冲击三观地得了第四呢~</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>86年世界杯，墨西哥成为<b>世界上第一个当了两次东道主的国家，</b>于是，他们又进了8强，不过这次参赛队有24个。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-19329a0bcd69828cdfd0610de2e09d23_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-19329a0bcd69828cdfd0610de2e09d23_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;610&#39; height=&#39;250&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"610\" data-rawheight=\"250\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"610\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-29fedca4c7e3dce0b85cf899b07bbbb0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-29fedca4c7e3dce0b85cf899b07bbbb0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>墨西哥遭遇美国，不禁联想到特朗普要在两国漫长的边境线上修墙，过多的巧合，让我怀疑世界杯上的巧合真的只是巧合吗？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2006年，十六进八，终结者阿根廷</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9b66db46e1fbf3f4319be47d4c54d95f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"619\" data-rawheight=\"464\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"619\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9b66db46e1fbf3f4319be47d4c54d95f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;619&#39; height=&#39;464&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"619\" data-rawheight=\"464\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"619\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9b66db46e1fbf3f4319be47d4c54d95f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9b66db46e1fbf3f4319be47d4c54d95f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>那时梅西还是“小荷才露尖尖角”，巴蒂他们已经退役，主力是萨维奥拉他们，萨维奥拉又回河床了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-acc7a4d4ccac1d542c7dae8b86aae33a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"802\" data-rawheight=\"558\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"802\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-acc7a4d4ccac1d542c7dae8b86aae33a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;802&#39; height=&#39;558&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"802\" data-rawheight=\"558\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"802\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-acc7a4d4ccac1d542c7dae8b86aae33a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-acc7a4d4ccac1d542c7dae8b86aae33a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>萨维奥拉才是我们这代人的球星。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>南非世界杯，终结墨西哥的也是阿根廷，只不过这次是小组赛，梅西翅膀硬了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d16a3d00176d692b2561af8cdc0c9ca9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"580\" data-rawheight=\"373\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"580\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d16a3d00176d692b2561af8cdc0c9ca9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;580&#39; height=&#39;373&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"580\" data-rawheight=\"373\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"580\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d16a3d00176d692b2561af8cdc0c9ca9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d16a3d00176d692b2561af8cdc0c9ca9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>不过进球的是伊瓜因。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>上届世界杯，对荷兰，栽在终场前判罚的点球，又是十六进八。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-06bc630d39dc0ea1ae30f34adf789277_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"497\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-06bc630d39dc0ea1ae30f34adf789277_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;497&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"497\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-06bc630d39dc0ea1ae30f34adf789277_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-06bc630d39dc0ea1ae30f34adf789277_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>墨西哥不大，但有极强的文化软实力。而墨西哥人也有着很多同等发展水平国家少有的文化自信心。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d9bc7ba89715870f9c08dc4d2a5196b9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"860\" data-rawheight=\"485\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"860\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d9bc7ba89715870f9c08dc4d2a5196b9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;860&#39; height=&#39;485&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"860\" data-rawheight=\"485\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"860\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d9bc7ba89715870f9c08dc4d2a5196b9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d9bc7ba89715870f9c08dc4d2a5196b9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>俄罗斯世界杯上，他们洋溢着热情，向全世界展示他们的文化符号。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a1bdffe858984c52f5379df215c0ce69_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a1bdffe858984c52f5379df215c0ce69_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a1bdffe858984c52f5379df215c0ce69_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a1bdffe858984c52f5379df215c0ce69_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>打德国时，你们一定听到了球场上几千个喉咙唱出的<b>墨西哥民歌Canta y no llores</b> 《别哭，纵情歌唱》</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4d25db2a0496bb34714ffe3f9da595be_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"675\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4d25db2a0496bb34714ffe3f9da595be_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;675&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"675\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4d25db2a0496bb34714ffe3f9da595be_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4d25db2a0496bb34714ffe3f9da595be_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这首歌风靡整个西语世界，简直是代表墨西哥国家形象的“国歌”。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9103767c9bde904e50c49e300a69140c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"550\" data-rawheight=\"413\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"550\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9103767c9bde904e50c49e300a69140c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;550&#39; height=&#39;413&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"550\" data-rawheight=\"413\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"550\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9103767c9bde904e50c49e300a69140c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9103767c9bde904e50c49e300a69140c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>马德里太阳门广场就有一支Canta y no llores专业户。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>canta y no llores</b>来自Freedom西班牙<i>00:0004:17</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>别的不说，<b>来自墨西哥的农作物占领全世界的饭桌已经几个世纪了。</b></p><p>暂且不说近几年的网红牛油果，人畜友好的玉米、南瓜、西红柿、菜豆</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>没有墨西哥，就没有巧克力</b>，可可是曾经玛雅贵族的神圣饮品。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bd9028569bc4a749ab3569b274d6380b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"830\" data-rawheight=\"584\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"830\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bd9028569bc4a749ab3569b274d6380b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;830&#39; height=&#39;584&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"830\" data-rawheight=\"584\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"830\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bd9028569bc4a749ab3569b274d6380b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bd9028569bc4a749ab3569b274d6380b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>墨西哥尤卡旦半岛和危地马拉的<b>玛雅人</b>最先发现可可豆能放松心情</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6bac573f34e0945c49072c358533f97d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"788\" data-rawheight=\"632\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"788\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6bac573f34e0945c49072c358533f97d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;788&#39; height=&#39;632&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"788\" data-rawheight=\"632\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"788\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6bac573f34e0945c49072c358533f97d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6bac573f34e0945c49072c358533f97d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>他们制作的<b>巧克力饮品要加盐、胡椒、肉桂粉，还有玉米面、辣椒</b>，具体做法不一而足。想想就是充满激情的饮料。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-dadb9fb10a06643db66f16b126d202d8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"650\" data-rawheight=\"434\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"650\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-dadb9fb10a06643db66f16b126d202d8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;650&#39; height=&#39;434&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"650\" data-rawheight=\"434\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"650\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-dadb9fb10a06643db66f16b126d202d8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-dadb9fb10a06643db66f16b126d202d8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>尤卡旦半岛还有一个可可博物馆</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>贡献一个玛雅热巧克力的方子，4人份，找的齐配料你们可以试试：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-8bf3a772c50457c3c10cd8d3118bbacf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"620\" data-rawheight=\"465\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"620\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-8bf3a772c50457c3c10cd8d3118bbacf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;620&#39; height=&#39;465&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"620\" data-rawheight=\"465\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"620\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-8bf3a772c50457c3c10cd8d3118bbacf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-8bf3a772c50457c3c10cd8d3118bbacf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>1/2杯生可可豆</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>2个中等大小干辣椒</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>半勺肉桂粉</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>1/4杯玉米面</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>6-8杯水</p><p>蜂蜜（看心情，可以不加）</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>一句话总结下人家写了七八页的方子：</b>可可豆烘干，所有材料磨成粉，加冷水拌匀，煮开，加蜂蜜调味。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>有一部<b>墨西哥电影《巧克力情人》（我也是冲着片名才看的）</b>，以巧克力展开的19世纪末美食与爱的故事。原著被列入20世纪百强西班牙语小说。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-de1c826c763c41d7bb97f671fc547d3d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"570\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-de1c826c763c41d7bb97f671fc547d3d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;570&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"570\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-de1c826c763c41d7bb97f671fc547d3d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-de1c826c763c41d7bb97f671fc547d3d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>最小的女儿是用来当佣人使唤的，母亲去世前不能结婚。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c28b343d85dc5cc409f892a2c4a6992_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"575\" data-rawheight=\"323\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"575\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c28b343d85dc5cc409f892a2c4a6992_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;575&#39; height=&#39;323&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"575\" data-rawheight=\"323\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"575\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c28b343d85dc5cc409f892a2c4a6992_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c28b343d85dc5cc409f892a2c4a6992_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>为了爱她，他取了她二姐，<b>这男人其实挺渣的。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>另外，没有墨西哥就没有无辣不欢</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b1e6bd3751afd72e98abf7256d9d8a08_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"675\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b1e6bd3751afd72e98abf7256d9d8a08_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;675&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"675\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b1e6bd3751afd72e98abf7256d9d8a08_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b1e6bd3751afd72e98abf7256d9d8a08_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>无法想象，辣椒从墨西哥传到亚欧大陆之前四川人民的饮食结构。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>吃的事儿等会再展开说，讲讲<b>墨西哥灿烂的文明</b>。</p><p>哥伦布之前的美洲文明中有两个在墨西哥，<b>玛雅文明</b>（除了墨西哥还有危地马拉、洪都拉斯、萨尔瓦多和伯利兹）和<b>阿斯台克文明</b>。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>梅尔吉普森有一部电影《启示》</b>就是玛雅文明背景下，部落间的伙并和弱肉强食。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e60dd5fec37eacd88d8356699bac3bca_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"990\" data-rawheight=\"632\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"990\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e60dd5fec37eacd88d8356699bac3bca_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;990&#39; height=&#39;632&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"990\" data-rawheight=\"632\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"990\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e60dd5fec37eacd88d8356699bac3bca_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e60dd5fec37eacd88d8356699bac3bca_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>赤裸裸的生存竞争，抽丝剥茧，还原了人类社会最本质的样貌：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>你跑得慢，敌人就会灭了你。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18b2e96a617f6c1837f9b5e6f17c3589_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"704\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18b2e96a617f6c1837f9b5e6f17c3589_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;704&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"704\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18b2e96a617f6c1837f9b5e6f17c3589_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18b2e96a617f6c1837f9b5e6f17c3589_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>你累了，惦记你的人还在虎视眈眈。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a9dfa079b50ba72ec9bf1025ff323a96_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"852\" data-rawheight=\"480\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"852\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a9dfa079b50ba72ec9bf1025ff323a96_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;852&#39; height=&#39;480&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"852\" data-rawheight=\"480\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"852\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a9dfa079b50ba72ec9bf1025ff323a96_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a9dfa079b50ba72ec9bf1025ff323a96_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>亡我之心不死。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6a763d831e7e928ca447dcdf42e1609f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"672\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6a763d831e7e928ca447dcdf42e1609f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;672&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"672\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6a763d831e7e928ca447dcdf42e1609f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6a763d831e7e928ca447dcdf42e1609f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>最震撼影片里盛大的祭祀场景。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fbda710270cab244af0409f5c44d1d81_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1021\" data-rawheight=\"557\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1021\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fbda710270cab244af0409f5c44d1d81_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1021&#39; height=&#39;557&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1021\" data-rawheight=\"557\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1021\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fbda710270cab244af0409f5c44d1d81_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fbda710270cab244af0409f5c44d1d81_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>作为祭品的人被刷成蓝色，砍头扔下金字塔的画面，至今记忆犹新。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a82259d906083224da583754a5a0b811_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"716\" data-rawheight=\"474\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"716\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a82259d906083224da583754a5a0b811_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;716&#39; height=&#39;474&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"716\" data-rawheight=\"474\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"716\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a82259d906083224da583754a5a0b811_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a82259d906083224da583754a5a0b811_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>《启示》（源自希腊文Apocalypto，意为&#34;发现&#34;、&#34;揭示&#34;、&#34;文明的崩毁与重生&#34;）</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>人类社会本来就是虚拟的构建，我们把原本不存在的宫殿、教堂、琼楼玉宇从头脑里搬到现实中。<b>世界不过是少数实力强大玩家的游戏，普通人不过是他们手中的棋子。</b>连女娲造人也是心情好了用手捏，心情不好用泥水复制。女娲娘娘任性，开心是少数。好在，作为棋子的普通人也有普通人的温情。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f8669b826b10c3aa9d549f667e8e7c17_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"581\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f8669b826b10c3aa9d549f667e8e7c17_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;581&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"581\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f8669b826b10c3aa9d549f667e8e7c17_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f8669b826b10c3aa9d549f667e8e7c17_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>玛雅文明有金字塔，我见过洪都拉斯首都的1比1仿制品，也就两三层楼那么高吧。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>墨西哥的玛雅金字塔主要分布在尤卡旦半岛的 Chichén Itzá, Teotihuacán和Uxmal，显然比两三层楼更高。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-469d9a4e0e594ee2e1a2fc3d79919be9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"778\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-469d9a4e0e594ee2e1a2fc3d79919be9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;778&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"778\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-469d9a4e0e594ee2e1a2fc3d79919be9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-469d9a4e0e594ee2e1a2fc3d79919be9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>尤卡旦半岛的原著民，至今都讲玛雅语。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>玛雅人好战尚武，看电影就知道。<b>他们还是一群古老的商人。商业是玛雅社会的基石。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>主要交易品中有盐和奴隶。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a62d36e76c5f5621263fa9ba880c70bd_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"412\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"412\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;412&#39; height=&#39;600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"412\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"412\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a62d36e76c5f5621263fa9ba880c70bd_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>从考古出土推断，<b>玛雅商人衣着光鲜，来自精英阶级。</b>你们是怎么从上面这块古代的转画上看出精英的？瞬间感觉自己缺少发现美的眼睛。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c51580a051f9516db4b6cab2713ba818_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"636\" data-rawheight=\"318\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"636\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c51580a051f9516db4b6cab2713ba818_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;636&#39; height=&#39;318&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"636\" data-rawheight=\"318\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"636\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c51580a051f9516db4b6cab2713ba818_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c51580a051f9516db4b6cab2713ba818_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>西班牙殖民考古学家更是发现玛雅遗址中的集市，以此推断玛雅人已有商品经济。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>当然，玛雅人还有历法，有关于2012的预言。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7dd1094d88679fd1468f2eea61ca5905_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"598\" data-rawheight=\"338\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"598\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7dd1094d88679fd1468f2eea61ca5905_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;598&#39; height=&#39;338&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"598\" data-rawheight=\"338\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"598\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7dd1094d88679fd1468f2eea61ca5905_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7dd1094d88679fd1468f2eea61ca5905_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>玛雅太阳历，但是有点复杂，等我学会了再教你们看。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>说起墨西哥的另一个古文明，阿斯台克文明。讲讲<b>墨西哥国旗的故事</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>我一直觉得，国旗上的符号是一个国家最希望向外界展示的一面，也是最引以为豪的一面。所以，只要有机会，我都会问问外国人他们国家的国旗象征什么。算是迅速走进一个国家的窗口吧。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-522d1f75edbff5e19922a0b141980d87_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"580\" data-rawheight=\"331\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"580\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-522d1f75edbff5e19922a0b141980d87_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;580&#39; height=&#39;331&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"580\" data-rawheight=\"331\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"580\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-522d1f75edbff5e19922a0b141980d87_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-522d1f75edbff5e19922a0b141980d87_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>墨西哥国旗红绿白三色，白色部分有国徽，图案是嘴里叼着一条蛇停在仙人掌上的雄鹰。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这个国旗什么意思呢？</p><p>绿色，墨西哥民族的希望</p><p>白色，纯洁的理想</p><p>红色，烈士的鲜血</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>国徽包含了<b>墨西哥立国的传说：</b>阿斯台克文人是墨西哥原著民中主要一支，他们幸福生活在一个叫阿斯特兰的地方，后来他们的主神Huitzilopochtli告诉他们要远走他方，直到看见<b>雄鹰叼着蛇落在仙人掌的地方，那里就是他们的家。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7706d2ae7af9da3e7a0bd1d18056f8f9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"676\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7706d2ae7af9da3e7a0bd1d18056f8f9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;676&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"676\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7706d2ae7af9da3e7a0bd1d18056f8f9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7706d2ae7af9da3e7a0bd1d18056f8f9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>320年后，他们找到了那个叫特诺奇蒂特兰城的地方。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fbee09c7e0c75d570c97b26a249e47df_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"567\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fbee09c7e0c75d570c97b26a249e47df_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;567&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"567\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fbee09c7e0c75d570c97b26a249e47df_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fbee09c7e0c75d570c97b26a249e47df_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>于是就有了今天的墨西哥</b></p><p>十分惭愧，至今没去过墨西哥。对墨西哥的了解主要来自影视作品和墨西哥同学、老师、同事和客户。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>说起<b>墨西哥电影和电视剧</b>，我要来如数家珍了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>墨西哥传媒巨头Televisa是西班牙语世界最大的传媒公司，主要从事影视剧制作，当然也做电影、电台、广告、互联网……</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-68b9573392786ff0fcc2b044ed57fa0f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-68b9573392786ff0fcc2b044ed57fa0f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;450&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"450\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"450\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-68b9573392786ff0fcc2b044ed57fa0f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-68b9573392786ff0fcc2b044ed57fa0f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>那些年<b>打着学西语的旗号追的每一部堪比韩剧的拉美肥皂剧</b>，必有Televisa的logo。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>大三那年，西班牙国家电视台热播的Mar de amor</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c35ad016143a0f53ba3dc4ecc46e3abb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"598\" data-rawheight=\"314\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"598\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c35ad016143a0f53ba3dc4ecc46e3abb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;598&#39; height=&#39;314&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"598\" data-rawheight=\"314\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"598\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c35ad016143a0f53ba3dc4ecc46e3abb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c35ad016143a0f53ba3dc4ecc46e3abb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>灰姑娘+高富帅的组合</b>，很符合韩剧毁人不倦的逻辑，市场需求所在，<b>Televisa电视剧的主要受众是大妈和家庭主妇。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>Camaleones,打着学习的旗号追的另一部墨西哥剧</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2908b140371bc3dc04e980e6eabc3d27_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"676\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2908b140371bc3dc04e980e6eabc3d27_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;676&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"676\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2908b140371bc3dc04e980e6eabc3d27_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2908b140371bc3dc04e980e6eabc3d27_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>算是青春偶像剧，除了高富帅+灰姑娘，</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9e11bf2d62d15245d17fac6707510826_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"370\" data-rawheight=\"544\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"370\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;370&#39; height=&#39;544&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"370\" data-rawheight=\"544\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"370\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9e11bf2d62d15245d17fac6707510826_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>还有校长女儿白富美倒追穷小子的桥段</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3f373a242e0aa70523a94ecf8724b2a7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"682\" data-rawheight=\"1023\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"682\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3f373a242e0aa70523a94ecf8724b2a7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;682&#39; height=&#39;1023&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"682\" data-rawheight=\"1023\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"682\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3f373a242e0aa70523a94ecf8724b2a7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3f373a242e0aa70523a94ecf8724b2a7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>还有事儿逼兮兮的教导主任</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-48ed4ab5467d1d78d3d5d804ea013772_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"685\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-48ed4ab5467d1d78d3d5d804ea013772_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;685&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"685\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-48ed4ab5467d1d78d3d5d804ea013772_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-48ed4ab5467d1d78d3d5d804ea013772_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>和黑帮元素，墨西哥犯罪率还是很可观的</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-60178ebfcff5f65f679ce671aab144b6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"562\" data-rawheight=\"501\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"562\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-60178ebfcff5f65f679ce671aab144b6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;562&#39; height=&#39;501&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"562\" data-rawheight=\"501\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"562\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-60178ebfcff5f65f679ce671aab144b6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-60178ebfcff5f65f679ce671aab144b6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>推荐一些墨西哥题材的电影</b><br/><br/>年初大热的<b>《寻梦环游记》</b>，以鬼节，墨西哥“清明节”为背景。<b>有时真心惊叹世界各地的人类文明的相似之处。</b><br/><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2b9bda3e69377f02f4c59375dcf856cd_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2b9bda3e69377f02f4c59375dcf856cd_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;608&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"608\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2b9bda3e69377f02f4c59375dcf856cd_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2b9bda3e69377f02f4c59375dcf856cd_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><br/><br/>西班牙的好莱坞女星佩内洛普.克鲁兹主演的《侠盗魅影》历史题材，19世纪末，两个来自不同阶级的墨西哥少女跟掠夺农民土地的美国人斗智斗勇的故事。<br/><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7b1e98f1e59e0a873c27cfaae22d3cfc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"502\" data-rawheight=\"402\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"502\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7b1e98f1e59e0a873c27cfaae22d3cfc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;502&#39; height=&#39;402&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"502\" data-rawheight=\"402\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"502\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7b1e98f1e59e0a873c27cfaae22d3cfc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7b1e98f1e59e0a873c27cfaae22d3cfc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><br/><br/><b>双女主的电影，还是首推《末路狂花》。</b><br/><br/>关于越过边境到美国讨生活的墨西哥移民。曾经有个墨西哥同事，感觉他骨子里好勇斗狠，杀气腾腾。后来听他讲自己曾经如何从墨西哥偷渡到美国，<b>有过那样一段经历的人，更理解生存是什么意思。并不是每个人都有成为好人的幸运。</b><br/><br/>Padre nuestro，《我们的父亲》，看完很揪心的一部电影。<b>不牵扯利益，谁都可以是好人；生死攸关，谁也都可以是坏人。</b><br/><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b100c533c6250ce77fa80a2d898d4754_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"576\" data-rawheight=\"350\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"576\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b100c533c6250ce77fa80a2d898d4754_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;576&#39; height=&#39;350&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"576\" data-rawheight=\"350\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"576\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b100c533c6250ce77fa80a2d898d4754_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b100c533c6250ce77fa80a2d898d4754_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><br/><br/>La misma luna《同一个月亮下》，一个墨西哥小男孩用自己的零用钱偷渡到美国找妈妈<br/><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a5df82f1b67d9d3ece037de0dce93b19_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"720\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a5df82f1b67d9d3ece037de0dce93b19_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;620&#39; height=&#39;445&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"620\" data-rawheight=\"445\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"620\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b11acb6d85ad23ee368c2fe461178281_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b11acb6d85ad23ee368c2fe461178281_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这只球队的背景比较国际化，分别来自葡萄牙、美国、瑞典和哥斯达黎加本国等多个国家的俱乐部。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>还记得那年，中国队打进世界杯。</b></p><p>哥斯达黎加是中国队第一个世界杯对手。那时候我上初一，正好考试季下午上自习，带了个小收音机到学校，耳机藏在头发里边（幸亏头发多），假装学习听了一下午比赛。班主任睁一只眼闭一只眼。也许这也就是为什么大学以后我不再关注足球，因为看球从学霸特权变成了大众娱乐，更少了跟班主任斗智斗勇的快感。一番自我心理分析后，发现自己还是挺阴暗的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>回忆下当年那支中国队尘封在记忆里的面孔。李玮锋、李铁，哥队那个9号叫什么来着？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-23e4b6d9c96b5e6689a6144adcbb3686_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"344\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-23e4b6d9c96b5e6689a6144adcbb3686_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;586&#39; height=&#39;344&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"344\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-23e4b6d9c96b5e6689a6144adcbb3686_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-23e4b6d9c96b5e6689a6144adcbb3686_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>进第一个球的戈麦斯，现在危地马拉一个俱乐部执教。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-dd3e023e54a03a43e6767ce7cb6dec96_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"612\" data-rawheight=\"441\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"612\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-dd3e023e54a03a43e6767ce7cb6dec96_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1024&#39; height=&#39;576&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"576\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7e42f5e6c3a916a81bea1949cca0431a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7e42f5e6c3a916a81bea1949cca0431a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>还有当年的主力前锋9号万乔普，想当年还在西甲马拉加踢过。当然也在曼城踢过，但是作为曾经的马拉加村民，有义务推广一下我们村的光辉形象。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-35350eccc35ff4566780936de8853d95_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"823\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-35350eccc35ff4566780936de8853d95_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4dbbbd2fbfba9b5a5d8873816a930bee_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4dbbbd2fbfba9b5a5d8873816a930bee_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>哥斯达黎加还是好几届中美洲杯冠军。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dcb2cd23234046c367978e9def4ba003_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"492\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dcb2cd23234046c367978e9def4ba003_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;492&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"492\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dcb2cd23234046c367978e9def4ba003_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-dcb2cd23234046c367978e9def4ba003_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>中美洲都有哪些国家？赶紧看看图，万一专八考了呢~</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-ac0f3f93b2f86f09470a0540141e8b71_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"720\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-ac0f3f93b2f86f09470a0540141e8b71_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;960&#39; height=&#39;720&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"720\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-ac0f3f93b2f86f09470a0540141e8b71_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-ac0f3f93b2f86f09470a0540141e8b71_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>科普一个西班牙人也经常跳进去的坑：西班牙语里哥斯达黎加人怎么说？</p><p><b>不是costarriqueño，而是costarricense</b></p><p>我女人大学毕业后第一份工作是在哥斯达黎加，我们当时都说她马上要变成costarriqueña了，外教说应该是costarricense，我们都中了波多黎各人是puertorriqueño的毒。</p><p><b>这段不学西语的人可以省略。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>女人说，哥斯达黎加是一个没有冬天的地方，她在异乡的第一个春节是在一片盛夏中度过。为了营造国内过年隆冬的氛围，他们把空调开到最低，裹着被子说：“真冷啊~”</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>女人讲过哥国的海滩很蓝、很美，她和另一个人肩并着肩在洒满月光的海滩上散步。然后就没有然后了。。。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>从她那儿盗了一些图</p><p>Villa Galita</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-90766878986a17bbd7afc53bc063e1e7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"720\" data-rawheight=\"540\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"720\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-90766878986a17bbd7afc53bc063e1e7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;720&#39; height=&#39;540&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"720\" data-rawheight=\"540\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"720\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-90766878986a17bbd7afc53bc063e1e7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-90766878986a17bbd7afc53bc063e1e7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cedc006032c6e7a3eb512f80255ca08d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"768\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cedc006032c6e7a3eb512f80255ca08d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1024&#39; height=&#39;768&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1024\" data-rawheight=\"768\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1024\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cedc006032c6e7a3eb512f80255ca08d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cedc006032c6e7a3eb512f80255ca08d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>Iglesia Nuestra Señora de los Ángeles，哥国很有名的教堂，据说圣母曾在此现身。《茶馆》里的名言：勿议国事，说到宗教，拉美人民多是虔诚的天主教徒，中美洲的小国和梵蒂冈的关系错综复杂，也算他们跟我国没有建交的原因之一吧。不过，话说有奶就是娘，去年巴拿马抛弃了台湾，而哥斯达黎加更是2007年就跟我国建交，是中美洲国家里觉悟比较早的。而第一个跟我们建交的中美洲国家是尼加拉瓜（1985年），我女人也待过。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-17b44bbae1453ed865ae0b9e1dcd3544_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"750\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-17b44bbae1453ed865ae0b9e1dcd3544_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "content": "<p>学过西语的人，对秘鲁都有这么点儿向往。<b>马丘比丘、纳斯卡地画、古老的印加帝国……</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>先说说世界杯上这只秘鲁队，猜你们也不是很了解，我来<b>现学现卖</b>了。</p><p>俄罗斯之前，<b>秘鲁国家队已经36年没有打进世界杯决赛阶段了，</b>而中国队是16年。。。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2cb2f2275a2fb545047fd7803cf07857_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"540\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2cb2f2275a2fb545047fd7803cf07857_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
